medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" data-eq-state="xsmall"><div class="cd__wrapper" data-analytics="_carousel-large-strip_article_"><div class="media"><a href="/2016/02/10/health/marijuana-weed-verbal-memory/index.html" onclick="CNN.Analytics.utils.clickEventTracker(event, 'hpt=cGFnZV80Y29sX2hlYWx0aF9zZWN0aW9uIGZyb250X3pvbmUtMC03X0luIENhc2UgWW91IE1pc3NlZCBJdF9jbi1jb250YWluZXJfMkYzOTc3OEYtMEFENS0zMjRDLURFM0MtM0NEM0MzNTQwQzlDX25vLXZhbHVlLXNldA==;hpt2=cGFnZV80Y29sX2hlYWx0aF9zZWN0aW9uIGZyb250X3pvbmUtMC03X2JhbGFuY2VkX2NuLWNvbnRhaW5lcl8yRjM5Nzc4Ri0wQUQ1LTMyNEMtREUzQy0zQ0QzQzM1NDBDOUNfY2Fyb3VzZWw6bGFyZ2U=')"><img class="media__image media__image--responsive owl-lazy" alt=" GO WITH AFP STORY by Desiree Martin A picture taken on April 12, 2013 shows plants of marijuana at the plantation of the Sibaratas Med Can association in Mogan on the southwest coast of the island of Gran Canaria. The plants grow from cuttings for approximately two months and then blossom before being harvested, dried, stored in jars for a month and later processed to be consumed on site. Spanish law prohibits the possession of soft drugs like cannabis in public and its growth to be sold for profit is illegal. But the law does tolerate growing cannabis for personal use and its consumption in private. Dozens of private marijuana smoking clubs operate across Spain that take advantage of this legal loophole that serve cannabis users who do not want to get their drugs from the streets. Spanish law prohibits the possession of soft drugs like cannabis in public and its growth to be sold for profit is illegal. class="media__image media__image--responsive owl-lazy" alt="FILE - In this March 21, 2007, file photo, then-Missouri redshirt freshman Michael Keck, left, listens to a coach during defensive drllls at Faurot Field in Columbia, Mo. Keck, who transferred to Missouri State in 2009, played just two years of college football before he was knocked out and gave the sport up for good. He turned combative, began to struggle in school, and soon was spending most of his time indoors in a darkened room. Keck died in 2013 at age 25 of what doctors believe was an unrelated heart condition. His brain, as he requested, was donated to the Boston University lab researching a degenerative brain condition frequently found in contact-sport athletes. It was found that Keck had chronic traumatic encephalopathy, which had advanced to a stage never before seen in someone so young. (AP Photo/L.G.
